Help Improve the Translation
<@ID=window_txt-3-txt_@>
This game is developed by a single developer and has been in development for over four years.
The development workload is heavy, and not enough time has been invested in localization.
If you find any translation errors, please feel free to point them out.
Email: [loomingxu@qq.com].
Thank you very much!

# Shelf Notes:
Set the “<color=#F4CC51>Planned Stock</color>”, and residents will <color=#4AB04A>actively</color> move items here.
This is the biggest difference between a Shelf and a “Large Storage Chest” or “Material Pile”, which can only passively receive items.

Gameplay Guide
<@ID=window_txt-151100-txt_@>
This is a magical land—barren yet rich, silent yet perilous.
Do not recklessly provoke monsters.
Do not let residents run around aimlessly and waste time.
The less time residents spend walking, the more time they spend producing.
Do not expand the population excessively; too many people truly cannot be fed.
Keeping a certain ratio of large beds to small beds can stabilize the population range.
Monsters and enemies grow stronger with each respawn wave—the more you fight, the stronger they get.

<@ID=window_txt-313700-txt_@>

<@ID=window_txt-313800-txt_@>
Oracle: Popular in the Shang and Zhou periods over 3600 years ago, it is the earliest discovered mature writing system in China, the origin of Chinese characters. Named after its inscriptions on turtle shells and animal bones.
Approximately 4500 single characters have been discovered, and about 2000 characters have been deciphered. To decipher Oracle Bone Script, the Chinese Character Museum even issued a reward of 100,000 yuan for each character.
<@ID=window_txt-313900-txt_@>
Seal Script: After Emperor Qin Shi Huang unified the six states in 221 BC, he implemented the policy of "uniform writing, standard carts" to simplify and standardize characters.
<@ID=window_txt-314000-txt_@>
Regular Chinese characters: Chinese characters evolved from Oracle Script, Great Seal Script, Seal Script, and Clerical Script into regular script. Traditional characters are mainly used in Taiwan, Hong Kong, etc. Mainland China simplified traditional characters to form simplified Chinese characters, which are still in use today. Learning Chinese characters, writing them, and connecting with the ancients, this is a great fortune.
<@ID=window_txt-314100-txt_@>
Pictographs are evolved from picture writing, representing what the ancients saw, heard, thought, and imagined. Through these characters, we vaguely see the beginnings of our ancestors' civilization and recall our own childhood, learning to walk and speak.
<@ID=window_txt-314200-txt_@>
Qin Dynasty (221 BC - 207 BC) was the first unified feudal dynasty in China, originating from the state of Qin during the Spring and Autumn period and Warring States period. The ancestors of the Qin people were descendants of Emperor Huang's grandson, Zhuangxu, granted the Ying surname by Emperor Shun.
In 361 BC, Qin Xiaogong ascended the throne, heavily relying on Shang Yang's reforms, which promoted economic development and strengthened the military, making Qin the most powerful state during the late Warring States period.
Qin King Ying Zheng conquered Han, Zhao, Wei, Chu, Yan, and Qi, completing the unification of China. In 221 BC, Ying Zheng declared himself Emperor, known as the "First Emperor of Qin."
The Qin Dynasty established a centralized system with three ministers and nine officials, abolished the feudal system in favor of the county system, and unified weights, measures, and writing. The centralization of power laid the foundation for China's political system for over 2000 years.
<@ID=window_txt-314300-txt_@>
Han Dynasty (202 BC - 220 AD) succeeded the Qin Dynasty and was another unified dynasty, divided into Western and Eastern Han periods, lasting 405 years. The imperial family’s surname was Liu, hence it is also known as the Liu Han Dynasty.
The Han Dynasty was the most advanced civilization and powerful empire of the time, stretching its territory from Korea to Vietnam, over the Congling Mountains to the Mongolian Plateau. After the Han Dynasty, the Huaxia people gradually became known as the Han people, and their writing system as Chinese characters.
<@ID=window_txt-314400-txt_@>
The dragon is a mythical animal in ancient Chinese mythology, usually without wings but capable of flying. Dragons are skilled in transformation and can summon wind and rain, considered auspicious alongside the phoenix and qilin, and symbolizing imperial power.
The Chinese dragon is a product of agricultural civilization, responsible for ensuring favorable weather and carrying auspicious meanings such as bravery and good fortune.
Western dragons are a product of maritime civilization, often found in the eastern Mediterranean and ancient Greece, causing storms, spewing fire, and eating people. They are typically seen as symbols of evil.

<@ID=window_txt-314402-txt_@>
1. Each character has three ancient forms and one pictorial form, totaling four variations
2. Click the card, and if you consecutively view the same character’s form four times, the character is successfully deciphered
3. Deciphering all characters in the same batch will complete the game

<@ID=window_txt-314701-txt_@>
On this ancient land,
the mysterious Totem Pillar stands between heaven and earth,
sealing the Demon King who once destroyed the world.
The power of the ancient god flows within the totem,
and you—“<color=#4CB34C>Lord’s Soul</color>”
—are the eternal guardian of this territory,
sharing the endless divine power within the Totem Pillar,
and bearing the responsibility of maintaining this world.
<@ID=window_txt-314800-txt_@>
From the weathered carvings upon the Totem Pillar, we learn:
A thousand years ago, the ancient gods defeated the Demon King and sealed him within the Totem Pillar.
The gods promised the King and his heirs that if they would guard the Totem Pillar,
they would be granted divine power. Even if their flesh decayed, their souls would gain eternal life.
Their souls would reside within the Lord’s Aura,
ruling this continent forever alongside each successor of their lands.
<@ID=window_txt-314900-txt_@>
Through continuous deciphering of ancient texts, we learned:
As the Totem Pillar lacks maintenance and falls into disrepair over time, the dark power of the sealed Demon King will gradually seep into the land, giving rise to various monsters that plague the world. At the same time, the power of the Lord’s Aura will also gradually weaken.
Properly guarding the Totem Pillar will grant powerful Lord’s Aura strength—this is the promise of the ancient god.

Dear Lord:
Allow us to express our greetings. We have no ill intentions but would like to remind you of a fact: being with you, this beautiful lady is terribly unlucky.
To be honest, your character and abilities fall far short of hers, like a candle next to a gem. We do not understand why she chose you to be with. She is beautiful, wise, and visionary, while you are crude and shallow.
We sincerely advise you to let her go, for her own happiness. You are not worthy of her.
— From a Gentleman of Gunpowder City

<@ID=window_txt-349500-txt_@>
<color=#4CB34C>Trading Post</color>: Can accommodate traveling merchants who bring seeds, animals, and miscellaneous goods, though in limited quantities.
<color=#4CB34C>Border Trade Outpost</color>: Can accommodate merchants from the four directions (East, West, North, South) for large-scale trade. Buying out a certain item will cause them to carry double the amount next time.
<color=#4CB34C>Reception Desk</color>: Can accommodate various travelers passing through, providing them with accommodation and entertainment, yielding a good profit. They are willing to pay a high premium for the items they need.
<color=#4CB34C>Maritime Trade</color>: Build ships to sail out and directly procure materials from their origin at low prices. By bypassing middlemen, goods can also be sold at a good price.
<color=#4CB34C>Subordinate Territory</color>: After obtaining a subordinate territory, raw materials can be procured at very favorable prices, a privilege of large lords.

<@ID=build-103012-guide_info_@>
Caravan Station enables efficient transport of goods
# Requirements: There must be an adult horse in the Pasture, a carriage must be crafted at the Crafting Station, and a caravan route must be drawn
# If the route endpoint is not at a Caravan Station, the carriage will shuttle back and forth along that route
# Once the requirements are met, the Cart Driver will place the carriage and horse at the Caravan Station, then perform transport tasks along the designated route
Even when <color=#EE4242>hungry and starving</color> during transport, the Cart Driver will still try their best to deliver the cargo.
While loading and unloading, the Cart Driver will also look for cooked food to eat; you can prepare some for them.
# At the Caravan Station, set which items can be transported along this route.
# When the carriage departs, it evaluates demand along the route and loads goods from the Caravan Station.
# As it passes facilities, the Cart Driver unloads goods to replenish the facilities’ <color=#EE4242>Planned Stock</color>. At the same time, they load <color=#EE4242>excess items</color> from those facilities onto the carriage.
# After returning to the Caravan Station, all remaining goods on the carriage are unloaded into the station.
# In the Caravan Station, you can set whether to use manpower to move out excess items or move in planned items.
<@ID=build-103012-build_tips_@>
Construction operation: Click on the ground, and use the mouse to draw a frame to set the Caravan Station size. <color=#EE4242>Can rotate before drawing the frame.</color>
<@ID=build-103009-guide_info_@>
Use a magic-powered ice cellar to store food and preserve it indefinitely.
Consumes sapphire monthly to operate.
When no food is available, residents will take from the ice cellar.
Due to being buried underground, transportation of goods is difficult, and it's used for emergency storage of excess perishable items.
<@ID=build-109005-guide_info_@>
# After storing items in the Treasury, residents will be <color=#EE4242>forbidden</color> to take them, and they also <color=#EE4242>cannot be used for trade</color>
# Diplomacy or tribute will use items from the Treasury
# When adjusting Planned Stock, Porters will move items in or out

<@ID=build-103004-guide_info_@>
# Traveling merchants trade here. Different caravans offer different types and quantities of tradable items
# <color=#EE4242>Set Trade Stock</color>, and residents will move the specified quantity of items to the Trading Post. When the merchant arrives, you can sell these items and purchase the merchant’s goods.
# For some items, caravans are willing to <color=#EE4242>pay a premium</color>. For others, they will only <color=#EE4242>buy at a low price</color>.
# If an item from the caravan sells out, the quantity carried next time will increase
# Trade process:
[1] Set Planned Stock, residents move items in
[2] Wait for the merchant to arrive
[3] In the trade screen, choose which merchant goods to buy on the left, and which of your goods to sell on the right
[4] Barter trade
<@ID=build-103005-guide_info_@>
A trade caravan from the specified direction will <color=#EE4242>regularly trade</color> here.
Unlike traveling merchants, the items traded at the border trade outpost are <color=#EE4242>fixed</color>.
The types of items differ by the four directions of the border.
If the desired items are available, the caravan will <color=#EE4242>purchase at a higher price</color>, otherwise, they will only offer a very low price.
If a merchant sells out of an item, the quantity will increase next time.
Different lords control different pricing rights for materials, and building good relationships or subjugating other lords can grant trade discounts.

Crops require sowing, watering, fertilizing, and harvesting steps to yield results. The higher the completion rate of each step, the higher the final yield.
Only after watering is completed will residents begin fertilizing.

<@ID=build-106001-guide_info_@>
The following are the default settings. You can <color=#EE4242>swap the left and right mouse buttons</color> in the settings interface.
【Selection and Movement】<sprite name="mouse_left"> <color=#EE4242>Left-click</color> on a soldier, then <sprite name="mouse_right"><color=#EE4242>Right-click</color> on the ground to <color=#EE4242>move the soldier</color>.
Ranged soldiers will <color=#4CB34C>attack while moving</color>.
If you <color=#EE4242>Right-click double</color> on the ground, it will stop soldiers from attacking enemies while moving.
【Adjust Selection】After selecting a soldier, <sprite name="mouse_right"><color=#EE4242>Right-click</color> on the soldier to select/unselect them.
【Deselect】After selecting a soldier, <sprite name="mouse_left">Left-click anywhere that is not the soldier's location to deselect them.
【Return to Camp】After selecting a soldier, <sprite name="mouse_right">Click on the barracks, and the soldier will return to the camp to stand by.
【Resupply】After selecting a soldier, <sprite name="mouse_left">Click on a storage box, and the soldier will move there to resupply.
【Combat】After selecting a soldier, <sprite name="mouse_left">Click near a monster, and the soldier will move there to <color=#EE4242>automatically attack</color> the monster.
【Single Select】<sprite name="mouse_left"><color=#EE4242>Left-click</color> on a soldier to select.
【Select All of a Type】<sprite name="mouse_left"><color=#EE4242>Left-click double</color> on a soldier to select all soldiers of the same type.
【Auto-Resupply】Soldiers will automatically resupply when standing by at the barracks.
【Group Formation】After selecting soldiers, <sprite name="keyboard_CTRL">Ctrl+Number key<sprite name="keyboard_1"><sprite name="keyboard_2"><sprite name="keyboard_3"><sprite name="keyboard_4"><sprite name="keyboard_5">
When soldiers are knocked unconscious, logistics soldiers will come to rescue them.
When soldiers die, logistics soldiers will collect the bodies and retrieve their weapons and armor.
Soldier levels depend on the weapons they use.

<@ID=event-1028-event_name_@>
Food Stocks Too Low
<@ID=event-1028-event_desc_@>
Food stocks are too low
<@ID=event-1028-window_info_@>
Residents are hungry and need to eat.
Each person (children and adults alike) consumes about <color=#EE4242>60 units</color> of food per year.
Different types of food restore the same amount of satiety.
Gathering Camps, Farmlands, and Orchards produce <color=#EE4242>vegetarian food</color>,
while Hunter Camps, Pastures, and Fishing Wharves produce <color=#EE4242>meat</color>.
Food can also be purchased through trade.
If residents eat <color=#EE4242>raw food</color> directly, they are prone to gastroenteritis.
Through cooking, ingredients can be processed into cooked food, improving food utilization.
Food production takes time; to avoid famine, a certain amount of food stock must be maintained.
<@ID=event-1029-event_name_@>
Clothing Stocks Too Low
<@ID=event-1029-event_desc_@>
Clothing stocks are too low
<@ID=event-1029-window_info_@>
Residents wear clothing to effectively resist the cold.
Clothing wears out over time, with each resident needing one piece of clothing per year on average.
Clothing production takes time, so to prevent residents from freezing due to a lack of clothing, maintain a sufficient clothing stock.

Different professions have different tool wear rates.
Tool crafting takes time, so maintain a certain tool reserve.

<@ID=event-1035-event_name_@>
How to Command Troops
<@ID=event-1035-window_info_@>
The following are default settings. In the settings menu, you can <color=#EE4242>swap left and right mouse button functions</color>.
[Box Select & Move] <sprite name="mouse_left"> <color=#EE4242>Left-click and drag</color> to select Soldiers, then <sprite name="mouse_right"><color=#EE4242>right-click</color> the ground to <color=#EE4242>move Soldiers</color>.
Ranged Soldiers will <color=#4CB34C>attack while moving</color>.
If you <color=#EE4242>double right-click</color> the ground, attacking enemies during movement will be disabled.
[Adjust Selection] After selecting Soldiers, <sprite name="mouse_right"><color=#EE4242>right-click</color> a Soldier to select/deselect that Soldier.
[Cancel Selection] After selecting Soldiers, <sprite name="mouse_left">left-click a non-Soldier area to cancel selection.
[Return to Barracks] After selecting Soldiers, <sprite name="mouse_right">click the Barracks to have Soldiers return and stand by.
[Resupply] After selecting Soldiers, <sprite name="mouse_left">click a Storage Chest and Soldiers will move there to resupply.
[Combat] After selecting Soldiers, <sprite name="mouse_left">click near monsters and Soldiers will move there and <color=#EE4242>automatically attack</color> monsters.
[Single Select] <sprite name="mouse_left"><color=#EE4242>Left-click</color> a Soldier to select.
[Select Type] <sprite name="mouse_left"><color=#EE4242>Double left-click</color> a Soldier to select all Soldiers of the same type.
[Auto Resupply] When Soldiers are standing by in the Barracks, they will automatically resupply as needed.
[Grouping] After selecting Soldiers, <sprite name="keyboard_CTRL">Ctrl + number keys <sprite name="keyboard_1"><sprite name="keyboard_2"><sprite name="keyboard_3"><sprite name="keyboard_4"><sprite name="keyboard_5">
# After Soldiers fall unconscious, Logistics Soldiers are responsible for rescue
# After Soldiers die, Logistics Soldiers are responsible for collecting bodies and recovering weapons and equipment
# Soldier level is determined by the weapon they use
<@ID=event-1036-event_name_@>
Education and Training
<@ID=event-1036-window_info_@>
After receiving education and training, children grow into educated residents who can <color=#EE4242>complete work tasks faster</color>.
Educated residents can also <color=#EE4242>increase output</color> in most jobs.
They gain more food when gathering, more leather and meat when hunting.
They gain more products when farming and more meat when slaughtering livestock.
They also gain more fish when fishing.
In processing, manufacturing, medicine making, cooking, and brewing, the same materials yield more products.
<@ID=event-1037-event_name_@>
Logistics Soldier
<@ID=event-1037-window_info_@>
On the battlefield, rescue, medical aid, and loot collection are all performed by Logistics Soldiers.
Logistics Soldiers can wear armor and withstand damage.
Logistics Soldiers <color=#EE4242>run faster</color> than other Soldiers.
In the “Barracks” facility interface, you can use “Military Orders” to adjust Logistics Soldiers’ behavior rules.
You need to recruit a certain number of Logistics Soldiers.
<@ID=event-1038-event_name_@>
Residents' Happiness Too Low
<@ID=event-1038-event_desc_@>
Notice: Residents' happiness is too low
<@ID=event-1038-window_info_@>
Residents start with 3 happiness stars, corresponding to a happiness value of 60.
Happiness changes when residents experience happy or unhappy events.
Click a resident and check their info panel to see the <color=#4CB34C>specific reasons</color>.
Eating <color=#4CB34C>fine food</color>, drinking alcohol, eating snacks (chocolate, honey), attending worship and prayer, seeing blooming flowers in flowerpots, etc., can <color=#EE4242>increase happiness</color>.
Receiving rewards, having an attractive spouse, and eating favorite fruits also increase happiness.

Character Traits

<@ID=event-1041-event_name_@>
Game Overview
<@ID=event-1041-window_info_@>
This is a village simulation game. Your main actions are:
<color=#EE4242>issuing construction tasks</color>, <color=#EE4242>assigning villagers to work</color>, and <color=#EE4242>leading troops in battle</color>.
Villagers will automatically produce and live according to your arrangements.
After being assigned to a <color=#EE4242>Large Bed</color>, married villagers will <color=#4CB34C>have children</color>, and the village population will continue to grow.
More population is not always better—<color=#EE4242>population is both a resource and a burden</color>.
Villagers will <color=#EE4242>age, fall ill, and die</color>, and also need to <color=#EE4242>eat, sleep</color>, and <color=#EE4242>wear clothes to stay warm</color>.
Wise Lord, your decisions determine the rise and fall of this territory.
<@ID=event-1043-event_name_@>
Solar Eclipse
<@ID=event-1043-window_info_@>
A solar eclipse is a rare astronomical phenomenon. When it occurs, night will last for several months.
Affected by dark magic, corpses on the ground will <color=#EE4242>turn into skeletons</color>.
<color=#EE4242>Graveyards</color> will spawn ghosts and skeletons.
The number of monsters appearing in ancient tombs will double.
At the same time, the <color=#4CB34C>number of gem fragments dropped by monsters will also double</color>.
During a solar eclipse, Werewolves are more prone to frenzy.
A solar eclipse can be triggered by sacrificing to the Dark God at the [Dark Altar].
<@ID=event-1044-event_name_@>
Drought
<@ID=event-1044-window_info_@>
Drought is a rare climate disaster.
During a drought, shallow water areas on the ground will turn into cracked dry land.
After the water dries up, fish and shrimp will be stranded on the ground, and residents will eagerly pick up the catch, <color=#4CB34C>increasing their walking speed</color>.
After the drought ends, all dry land will return to shallow water, but fishery resources in the water will take years to fully recover.
You can sacrifice to the Dark God at the [Dark Altar] to trigger a drought.
<@ID=event-1045-event_name_@>
Combat Controls
<@ID=event-1045-window_info_@>
After box-selecting Soldiers, click near monsters and Soldiers will move over and <color=#EE4242>automatically attack</color> them.
For more Soldier-related operations, click the “Barracks” window title to view detailed instructions.
<@ID=event-1046-event_name_@>
Field Harvest Incomplete
<@ID=event-1046-window_info_@>
When winter arrives, if crops are not harvested in time, they will freeze to death, reducing farmland yield.
Pay attention to whether the <color=#EE4242>number of Farmers assigned</color> to farmland is sufficient.
Also note whether Farmers spend <color=#EE4242>too much time</color> on <color=#4CB34C>transporting and walking</color>.
<@ID=event-1047-event_name_@>
Baby Boom
<@ID=event-1047-window_info_@>
Excessive promotion of childbirth will lead to a short-term population explosion. This can easily cause a <color=#EE4242>food shortage</color>.
Additionally, a baby boom corresponds to a future <color=#EE4242>elderly boom</color>, resulting in a significant loss of labor in the short term.
Such sudden population changes are likely to <color=#EE4242>cause a collapse</color>.
You can control the population growth speed by adjusting the <color=#EE4242>number of large beds</color> and temporarily halting the use of some large beds.
<@ID=event-1048-event_name_@>
Logistics System Explanation
<@ID=event-1048-window_info_@>
Large Storage Chest, Material Pile, Transit Crate, Shelf, and Caravan Station form the core logistics system.
# <color=#4CB34C>Large Storage Chest and Material Pile</color> are used to <color=#EE4242>passively</color> receive items nearby.
# <color=#4CB34C>Transit Crate</color> takes up little space. It can receive items nearby and can also be set up to distribute specific items for specific professions.
# <color=#4CB34C>Shelf</color> requires setting a stock plan and will <color=#EE4242>actively</color> centralize stored goods for use by specialized workers.
# <color=#4CB34C>Caravan Station</color> has very high transport efficiency, especially suitable for long-distance, large-volume transport.
Residents’ hauling rules:
1. If a resident is carrying items, they will place them at the nearest storage facility that can accept the item
2. Residents will take production materials and personal supplies from the nearest <color=#4CB34C>Large Storage Chest, Material Pile, Transit Crate, Shelf</color>
3. Products from production facilities will be transported by Laborers to nearby storage facilities. After linking with a Caravan Station, products can be carried out by carriage.
4. If the entrances/exits (<color=#4CB34C>green arrows</color>) of a production facility and a storage facility overlap, a “link” is formed. Residents will prioritize storing products in the linked storage facility, reducing hauling actions.
5. After setting Planned Stock in the Treasury, items will be searched for anywhere and transported in
# Special case: After linking production facilities (Cooking Station, Crafting Station) with a Shelf, even if the Shelf is not set to accept the corresponding products, residents will still place the products on the Shelf
Suggestion:
Residents’ production involves a lot of walking and hauling. Through合理的 building layout, <color=#4CB34C>reducing walking and hauling during production can effectively improve work efficiency</color>.
<@ID=event-1049-event_name_@>
Collection Task Automatically Canceled
<@ID=event-1049-window_info_@>
After issuing gathering tasks for surface “wood”, “stone”, and “iron ore” via box selection, if residents find that the <color=#EE4242>task location is unreachable</color> during execution, the corresponding task will be <color=#EE4242>automatically canceled</color>.
<@ID=event-1050-event_name_@>
Outdoor Structures Will Be Demolished
<@ID=event-1050-window_info_@>
On the <color=#EE4242>world map</color>, after clicking the icon of another region, the top half of your territory (the area above the boundary river) will switch to the corresponding region.
In this region, if it is your territory, the facilities will be restored when switching back from another region.
Otherwise, the facilities will be <color=#EE4242>forced to be removed</color>.
<@ID=event-1051-event_name_@>
Cold Wave
<@ID=event-1051-window_info_@>
Cold waves are a climate disaster. During a cold wave, cold temperatures will last until the spring of the next year, with temperatures about 10 degrees lower than usual.
It rarely occurs in warm southern regions but is common in northern regions.
The prolonged cold will not only test the people but will also freeze some monsters.
<@ID=event-1052-event_name_@>
Royal Tax
<@ID=event-1052-window_info_@>
The King levies taxes annually, based on population.
Populations under 100 are tax-exempt.
At 100 population, each person pays <color=#4CB34C>10 silver coins</color> per year.
At 500 population, each person pays <color=#4CB34C>20 silver coins</color> per year.
At 1000 population, each person pays <color=#4CB34C>50 silver coins</color> per year.
At 1500 population, each person pays <color=#4CB34C>100 silver coins</color> per year.
Taxes are converted into Silver and collected first through banks, then through the treasury.
If full taxes cannot be collected in a given year, the King will show mercy and grant exemptions.

<@ID=event-1101-event_name_@>
Resident Death
<@ID=event-1101-event_desc_@>
A resident has died!
<@ID=event-1101-window_info_@>
Over time, residents will age and <color=#EE4242>die naturally</color>.
They may also <color=#EE4242>freeze to death</color> if they cannot find warmth.
They may <color=#EE4242>starve to death</color> if they cannot find food.
They may <color=#EE4242>disease and die</color> if they cannot receive timely treatment.
They may <color=#EE4242>die in battle</color> if they are injured by enemies or monsters.
After death, if there is a cemetery, they will be buried there.
If there is no space in the cemetery, they will be temporarily stored in the Material Pile until there is space to bury them.
If residents cannot be buried, their family members will be deeply saddened.
<@ID=event-1102-event_name_@>
Resident Caught a Cold
<@ID=event-1102-event_desc_@>
A resident has caught a cold!
<@ID=event-1102-window_info_@>
Residents outdoors on rainy days without an umbrella may catch a cold.
On snowy days, wearing tattered clothes may also cause a cold.
A cold is a common illness and will heal on its own with timely bed rest.
If rest is neglected for a long time, the condition may worsen and lead to shock.
Umbrellas and clothes can be crafted at the <color=#4CB34C>Sewing Table</color>.
<@ID=event-1103-event_name_@>
Resident Contracted an Infectious Disease
<@ID=event-1103-event_desc_@>
A resident has contracted an infectious disease!
<@ID=event-1103-window_info_@>
An infectious disease is a serious threat to residents' health.
Once infected, it can be cured by taking medicine.
After infection, there is a probability that residents may go into <color=#EE4242>shock</color> or even <color=#EE4242>die</color>.
However, most residents can rely on their immunity to <color=#4CB34C>self-heal</color>.
Once cured, residents will have immunity for two years.
During the illness, the infected will periodically expel the infection source around them.
Others who come into contact with the infection source will also become infected.
The infection source will <color=#4CB34C>disappear automatically</color> after a period of time. Doctors will also actively <color=#4CB34C>clean it up</color>.
Doctors are less likely to become infected due to their good protective measures.
<@ID=event-1104-event_name_@>
Resident Contracted Gastroenteritis
<@ID=event-1104-event_desc_@>
A resident has contracted gastroenteritis!
<@ID=event-1104-window_info_@>
If residents eat <color=#EE4242>raw food</color> for a long time, it will lead to gastroenteritis.
Gastroenteritis must be treated by a doctor through <color=#EE4242>medication</color>.
If residents get sick and do not receive treatment for a long time, they may suddenly faint.
<@ID=event-1105-event_name_@>
A Child is Born
<@ID=event-1105-event_desc_@>
A child has been born!
<@ID=event-1105-window_info_@>
Before the age of 3, infants need to be fed and clothed by others and cannot get out of bed or move on their own.
As time passes by 1 year, residents age by 5 years.
Generally speaking, over their lifetime, Dwarf commoners can have up to 4 children, Nobles up to 6, and Lords up to 8. Other races vary slightly.

<@ID=event-1108-event_name_@>
Stone Golem
<@ID=event-1108-event_desc_@>
Obtained a Wisdom Gem, which can be used to summon a Stone Golem
<@ID=event-1108-window_info_@>
When giant trees wither, they may drop a ��Wisdom Gem.��
The ��Wisdom Gem�� can grant life to stone and is used to summon Stone Golems.
Stone Golems can perform miscellaneous tasks.
Stone Golems are immune to cold, hunger, and disease, and can work without rest.
After being knocked down by bomb attacks, Stone Golems can be recovered and turned back into ��Wisdom Gems.��
Summoning Stone Golems requires first building a ��Light Altar.��
<@ID=event-1109-event_name_@>
Ants Have Appeared
<@ID=event-1109-window_info_@>
A group of worker ants is searching for a nesting site.
Most of the time, ants are not enemies, and worker ants do not attack.
However, worker ants will dismantle buildings within the ant nest territory.
When worker ants are attacked, soldier ants will emerge from the nest.
<@ID=event-1110-event_name_@>
Lord Gameplay Overview
<@ID=event-1110-window_info_@>
The Lord is the manager of the territory.
Only after the Lord takes office can diplomacy and conquest be carried out.
The Lord can switch to combat mode and, with the effect of the <color=#4CB34C>Lord��s Aura</color>, become a powerful combat unit.
The Lord��s descendants are <color=#4CB34C>royal family members</color>, and only royal family members can succeed as the new Lord.
When there are no royal family members to inherit the Lordship, a bloodline Lord must be introduced from another territory.
The Lord and royal family members enjoy a privileged life, allowing them to retain more <color=#4CB34C>talent traits</color> and produce more offspring.

<@ID=tutorial-1-tutorial_desc_@>
First, let's assign jobs to the residents.
Move the mouse to the <color=#EE4242>bottom left corner</color> to access the job allocation panel,
Click the “<color=#EE4242>plus sign</color>” to increase the number of workers and begin their professional tasks.
<@ID=tutorial-4-tutorial_desc_@>
Build a gathering camp in the forest to gather wild vegetables and fruits,
This will help us survive the tough pioneering period.
<@ID=tutorial-5-tutorial_desc_@>
Once you assign Gatherers, the gathering camp will function properly.
<@ID=tutorial-3-tutorial_desc_@>
Assign gathering tasks to obtain more building and production materials:
Logs, stones, and iron ore.
<@ID=tutorial-1001-tutorial_desc_@>
Tasks can be prioritized for faster completion.
<@ID=tutorial-1002-tutorial_desc_@>
Cancel excessive tasks to allow residents time for other work.
<@ID=tutorial-6-tutorial_desc_@>
To resist the cold, a fire is needed. The winter here can freeze people to death.
<@ID=tutorial-10-tutorial_desc_@>
Build a large bed for couples, so they will consider having children.
<@ID=tutorial-21-tutorial_desc_@>
There are deer herds nearby; send hunters to hunt and get abundant leather and meat.
<@ID=tutorial-22-tutorial_desc_@>
You need to assign one hunter.
<@ID=tutorial-8-tutorial_desc_@>
Build a door in the direction where residents frequently move to reduce detours and save time.
<@ID=tutorial-28-tutorial_desc_@>
Fishing is an important source of meat.
The larger the water area near the fisherman’s dock, the higher the annual catch limit.
When building, you can <color=#EE4242>rotate</color> the facility to fit the terrain.
<@ID=tutorial-29-tutorial_desc_@>
You can assign up to four fishermen by default, but this limit can be freely adjusted in the Fishermen’s Wharf interface.
<@ID=tutorial-23-tutorial_desc_@>
Build a dirt road connecting the gathering camp to improve production efficiency.

Faith is power! Faith creates miracles!

You need to assign a prophet.

<@ID=tutorial-20-tutorial_desc_@>

<@ID=tutorial-30-tutorial_desc_@>

<@ID=tutorial-24-tutorial_desc_@>
Be aware that residents may defecate anywhere! Build toilets.
<@ID=tutorial-36-tutorial_desc_@>
Manure must be in compost bins to ferment into fertilizer.
Toilets and ranches are the main sources of manure, and placing compost bins nearby can save manure transport time.
<@ID=tutorial-39-tutorial_desc_@>
Sickness is inevitable, treat it promptly. If delayed, a small illness can become a serious one, even life-threatening.
<@ID=tutorial-40-tutorial_desc_@>
Medical beds are needed for patient treatment to speed up recovery.
Especially for those without beds, residents sleeping on the floor who fall ill and faint won’t find a medical bed in time, risking death.

<@ID=letter-5601-name_@>
Letter from the Royal Capital
<@ID=letter-5601-desc_@>
I have long sought to maintain the seal
and searched for a way to continue without further sacrifice.
But the seal is weakening, and time is no longer on our side.
As King, I can only order the sacrifices to continue.
If another path truly exists, I hope you will find it.
<@ID=letter-5701-name_@>
The King’s Private Letter
<@ID=letter-5701-desc_@>
I have seen the true nature of the contract.
It exchanges the eternal suffering of a few for the peace of the world.
It maintains order but denies humanity itself.
I choose to end it.
I bind the Demon King with my own soul in exchange for his limited freedom.
He will not destroy the world on his own, and I will no longer uphold the absolute order of the gods with royal power.
From this moment on,
the throne will no longer derive legitimacy from the gods.
The world will be judged by humanity itself.
I do not know if humanity can bear this world.
But if we dare not even try, the world will never change.
You have not been shaped by royal power.
If there is a path that can stand between order and chaos,
I hope it is you who will walk it.
<@ID=letter-5801-name_@>
Letter from the Barbarians
<@ID=letter-5801-desc_@>
My Lord,
The throne is vacant, and the kings are fighting.
The continent needs a new ruler.
We are willing to form an alliance with you.
Offering <color=#4CB34C>one million gold and a hundred fine horses</color> to show our sincerity.
We hope you will grant us a foothold in the North.
In front of the factions on the continent,
We will openly support you as the new king.
This is cooperation, not begging.

<@ID=note-1-note_content_@>
Sprites can serve as free laborers, unaffected by cold, working without rest.
<@ID=note-2-note_content_@>
Residents must be assigned professions to perform corresponding jobs.
<@ID=note-3-note_content_@>

<@ID=note-4-note_content_@>
The game speed has 4 levels, corresponding to 1x, 3x, 5x, and 10x speed.
<@ID=note-5-note_content_@>
Couples need to be assigned to a large bed to procreate.
<@ID=note-6-note_content_@>
The construction process is divided into three stages: clearing the ground (<color=#EE4242>Laborers</color> perform this), transporting materials, and construction.
<@ID=note-7-note_content_@>
The cold will continuously reduce the warmth value of the residents, and a fire source is the most effective way to alleviate it.
<@ID=note-8-note_content_@>
In this wilderness, the cold and hunger show no mercy to anyone.
<@ID=note-9-note_content_@>
